32.3.39	viṣṇoś śamyor yajñasyānta iti
32.3.40	viṣṇur vai yajñaḥ
32.3.41	antata eva yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
32.4.1	iṣṭo yajño bhṛgubhir draviṇodā yatibhir iti
32.4.2	yajñasya vā eṣa dohaḥ
32.4.3	yajñam evaitad duhe
32.4.4	tasya yajñasyeṣṭasya sviṣṭasya draviṇaṃ māgacchatv ity āśiṣam evāśāste
32.4.5	aṅgiraso me 'sya yajñasya prātaranuvākair ahauṣur ity āśiṣām evaiṣa dohaḥ
32.4.6	vasur yajño vasumān yajña iti vasumantam eva yajñaṃ kurute
32.4.7	tasya yajñasya vasor vasumato vasu māgacchatv ity āśiṣam evāśāste
32.4.8	somo retodhā iti
32.4.9	somo vai devānāṃ retodhāḥ
32.4.10	soma evāsmai retodhā reto dadhāti
32.4.11	tvaṣṭā rūpāṇāṃ vikarteti
32.4.12	tvaṣṭā vai rūpāṇāṃ vikartā
32.4.13	so 'smai rūpāṇi vikaroti
32.4.14	devānāṃ patnīr agnir gṛhapatir mithunaṃ yajamānasyeti
32.4.15	etad vai darśapūrṇamāsayor mithunam
32.4.16	darśapūrṇamāsayor eva mithunena mithunam ātman dhatte
32.4.17	tayor ahaṃ devayajyayā mithunena prajaniṣīyeti
32.4.18	pra prajayā pra paśubhir jāyate
32.4.19	yā vā etasya patnī saitaṃ saṃprati paścād āsītāgnir asyāḥ prajā nirdahet
32.4.20	yad āha patny eṣa te patni loka iti lokam evāsyai karoti
32.4.21	anirdāhuko 'syā agniḥ prajā bhavati
32.4.22	saṃ patnī patyā sukṛteṣu gacchatām iti
32.4.23	patnyā evaiṣa yajñasyānvārambhaḥ
32.4.24	saha svarge loke bhavataḥ
32.4.25	svāhā svāheṣṭebhyo vaṣaḍ aniṣṭebhya iti
32.4.26	sviṣṭiś ca vai duriṣṭiś ca yajñe saṃyatete
32.4.27	yasya sviṣṭir yajñaṃ yuvate sa vasīyān bhavati
32.4.28	yasya duriṣṭir yajñaṃ yuvate sa pāpīyān bhavati
32.4.29	sviṣṭyaivāsya yajñaṃ samardhayati
32.4.30	vasīyān bhavati
32.4.31	ayāś cāgne 'sy anabhiśastiś ceti
32.4.32	ayā vai nāmaivāgnes tanūḥ
32.4.33	ayā maryādhair yeṇeti khalu vā āhuḥ
32.4.34	yāṃ ca vidma yajñasya prāyaścittiṃ yāṃ ca na vidma
32.4.35	yaś ca yajñasya kriyate yaś ca na kriyate
32.4.36	tasyaiṣobhayasya prāyaścittiḥ
32.4.37	sarasvatyai veśabhaginyai svāheti
32.4.38	veśayamanaṃ vā etat
32.4.39	api ha vā enam ājīvanta upāsate
32.4.40	vācam asya brāhmaṇasya vā rājanyasya vopāsmaha iti
32.4.41	ya evaṃ veda
32.4.42	yajñasya tvā pramayābhimayonmayā pratimayā parigṛhṇāmīti
32.4.43	gāyatrī vai yajñasya pramā
32.4.44	triṣṭub abhimā
32.4.45	jagaty unmā
32.4.46	anuṣṭup pratimā
32.4.47	etāvanti vai chandāṃsi yajñaṃ vahanti
32.4.48	tair evainaṃ parigṛhṇāti
32.4.49	teṣv enaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
34.1.1	ekādaśinībhir yanti
34.1.2	prāṇā vā ekādaśinīḥ
34.1.3	prāṇeṣv eva tat pratitiṣṭhanto yanti
34.1.4	tad āhur yad ekādaśinībhir iyur ahāni vātiricyeran paśavo vā nottamenāhnottamaḥ paśus saṃpadyeteti
34.1.5	tad yad ekādaśinīkāmās syuḥ prathame māsy ekādaśinīm upeyur uttame ca
34.1.6	prāṇā vā ekādaśinī
34.1.7	prāṇān eva mukhataḥ pratipadyante
34.1.8	prāṇeṣv antataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
34.1.9	aindrāgnaḥ khalv evācyutaḥ paśus syāt
34.1.10	prāṇāpānau vā indrāgnī
34.1.11	prāṇāpānayor eva tat pratitiṣṭhanto yanti
34.1.12	tejo vā indrāgnī
34.1.13	tejasy eva tat pratitiṣṭhanto yanti
34.1.14	ojo vai vīryam indrāgnī
34.1.15	tejasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhanto yanti
34.1.16	indrāgnī sarvā devatāḥ
34.1.17	yad aindrāgnaḥ paśur bhavati sarvā eva tad devatāḥ prīṇanto yanti
34.1.18	yad aho rathaṃtaraṃ sāma syād āgneyaṃ tad ahaḥ paśum ālabheran
34.1.19	yad ahar bṛhadaindraṃ tad ahas tad vaindrāgna eva
34.1.20	yad aho rathaṃtaraṃ sāma syād āgnendraṃ tad ahaḥ paśum ālabheran
34.1.21	yad ahar bṛhad aindrāgnaṃ tad ahaḥ
34.1.22	tad anupūrvaṃ devate kalpayanti
34.1.23	yathāpūrvaṃ paśūn ālabhante
34.1.24	indrāgnibhyām eva yanti
34.1.25	bārhaspatyaṃ śitipṛṣṭhaṃ ṣaṣṭhe 'hann ālabhheran
34.1.26	brahma vai bṛhaspatiḥ
34.1.27	brahmaṇy eva tad yajñasyāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
34.1.28	bārhaspatyaḥ khalu vāva śitipṛṣṭho devatayā
34.1.29	dyāvāpṛthivyāṃ dhenuṃ saptame 'hann ālabheran prathame chandome
34.1.30	dyāvāpṛthivī vai yajñasya pratiṣṭhā
34.1.31	dyāvāpṛthivyor eva tad yajñasyāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
34.1.32	dyāvāpṛthivyā khalu vāva dhenur devatayā
34.1.33	vāyavyaṃ vatsam aṣṭame 'hann ālabheran madhyame chandome
34.1.34	prāṇo vai vāyuḥ
34.1.35	prāṇa eva tad yajñasyāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
34.1.36	vāyavyaḥ khalu vāva vatso devatayā
34.1.37	vāce pṛśniṃ navame 'hann ālabherann uttame chandome
34.1.38	vāg vai pṛśniḥ pratiṣṭhā
34.1.39	vācy eva tad yajñasyāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
34.1.40	vāgdevatyā khalu vāva pṛśnir devatayā
34.1.41	ādityāṃ vaśāṃ daśame 'hann ālabheran
34.1.42	iyaṃ vā aditiḥ
34.1.43	iyaṃ pratiṣṭhā
34.1.44	asyām eva tad yajñasyāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
34.1.45	ādityā khalu vāva vaśā devatayā
34.1.46	vaiśvakarmaṇam ṛṣabhaṃ mahāvratīye 'hann ālabheran
34.1.47	indro vai vṛtraṃ hatvā viśvakarmābhavat
34.1.48	prajāpatiḥ prajās sṛṣṭvā viśvakarmābhavat
34.1.49	saṃvatsaro viśvakarmety āhuḥ
34.1.50	yam imāḥ prajā anuprajāyanta iti
34.1.51	trirūpas syād ubhayata etaḥ
34.1.52	yat prathamaṃ rūpaṃ tenaindraḥ
34.1.53	yad dvitīyaṃ tena prājāpatyaḥ
34.1.54	yat tṛtīyaṃ tat saṃvatsarasya rūpam
34.1.55	indro vṛṣā
34.1.56	prajāpatir vṛṣā
34.1.57	saṃvatsaro 'sya vṛṣety āhuḥ
34.1.58	yam imāḥ prajā anuprajāyanta iti
34.1.59	tasmād ṛṣabhas syāt
34.2.1	asuryaṃ vā etasmād varṇaṃ kṛtvā teja indriyaṃ vīryaṃ prajā paśavo 'pakrāmanti
34.2.2	yasya yūpo virohati sa īśvara ījānaḥ
34.2.3	pāpīyān bhavati
34.2.4	tvāṣṭraṃ bahurūpam ālabheta
34.2.5	tvaṣṭā vai rūpāṇāṃ vikartā
34.2.6	tam eva bhāgadheyenopadhāvati
34.2.7	so 'smai teja indriyaṃ vīryaṃ prajāṃ paśūn punar upāvartayati
34.2.8	ārtiṃ vā ete niyanti yeṣāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyate
34.2.9	taṃ yad avavṛjeyuḥ krūrakṛtām ivaiṣāṃ lokas syāt
34.2.10	āhara daheti brūyuḥ
34.2.11	taṃ dakṣiṇārdhe vedyā nidhāya sarparājñyā ṛgbhis stuyuḥ
34.2.12	iyaṃ vai sarparājñī
34.2.13	asyā evainam adhisamīrayanti
34.2.14	tad āhur vyṛddhaṃ vā etad yat stutam ananuśastam iti
34.2.15	hotā prathamo dīkṣitānāṃ prācīnāvītaṃ kṛtvā mārjālīyaṃ parīyād yāmīr anubruvan sarparājñyā ṛcāṃ kīrtayan
34.2.16	iyaṃ vai sarpato rājñī
34.2.17	asyā evainam adhisamīrayanti
34.2.18	dhuvanty evainam etat
34.2.19	atho ny evāsmai hnuvate
34.2.20	tama iva vā ete niyanti yeṣāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyate
34.2.21	agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti
34.2.22	etāṃ somasya pratipadaṃ kurvīran
34.2.23	punata evātmānam
34.2.24	āyur evātman dadhate
34.2.25	atho jyotiṣmanta eva yanti
34.2.26	apratiṣṭhitā vā ete yeṣāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyate
34.2.27	rathaṃtarasāmaiṣāṃ somas syāt
34.2.28	iyaṃ vai pṛthivī rathaṃtaram
34.2.29	asyām eva pratitiṣṭhanti
34.3.1	yady akrītam apahareyur anyaḥ kretavyaḥ
34.3.2	yadi krītaṃ yo nediṣṭhaṃ syāt sa āhṛtyābhiṣutyaḥ
34.3.3	rājāhārāya tu kiṃ cid deyam
34.3.4	tenāsya sa parikrīto bhavati
34.3.5	yadi somaṃ na vindeyuḥ pūtīkān abhiṣuṇuyuḥ
34.3.6	yadi na pūtīkān ārjunāni
34.3.7	gāyatrī vai somam apāharac chyeno bhūtvā
34.3.8	tasya somarakṣir anuvisṛjya nakham acchinat
34.3.9	tato yo 'ṃśur amucyata sa pūtīko 'bhavat
34.3.10	ūtīkā vai nāmaite
34.3.11	yad ūtīkān abhiṣuṇvanty ūtim eva yajñāya kurvanti
34.3.12	indro vai vṛtram ahan
34.3.13	tasya yal lohitam āsīt tāny ārjunāni lohitatūlāny abhavan
34.3.14	atha yo grīvābhyaḥ pravṛḍhābhyo rasas samasravat tāny ārjunāni babhrutūlāny abhavan
34.3.15	somo vā eṣo 'surya iva tu
34.3.16	tasmān nābhiṣutyaḥ
34.3.17	pratidhuk ca prātaḥ pūtīkāś ca
34.3.18	dadhi madhyandine
34.3.19	pūtīkāś ca śṛtaṃ cāparāhṇe pūtīkāś ca
34.3.20	indriyeṇa vā eṣa somapīthena vyṛdhyate yasya somam apāharanti
34.3.21	sa oṣadhīś ca paśūṃś ca praviśati
34.3.22	yad etad ubhayam abhiṣuṇvanty oṣadhibhyaś caiva paśubhyaś cādhi somapīthaṃ punar avarunddhe
34.4.1	yadi somau saṃsutau syātāṃ mahati rātryāḥ prātaranuvākam upākuryāt
34.4.2	pūrva eva yajñaṃ pūrvo devatāḥ pūrvaś chandāṃsi vṛṅkte
34.4.3	vṛṣaṇvatīṃ pratipadaṃ kuryāt
34.4.4	indro vai vṛṣā
34.4.5	prātassavanād evaiṣām indraṃ vṛṅkte
34.4.6	tad āhuḥ savanamukhesavanamukhe kartavyeti
34.4.7	savanamukhāt savanamukhād evaiṣām indraṃ vṛṅkte
34.4.8	saṃveśāyopaveśāya gāyatryai chandase 'bhibhuve svāhā
34.4.9	saṃveṣāyopaveśāya triṣṭubhe jagatyā anuṣṭubhe chandase 'bhibhuve svāheti
34.4.10	etāvanti vai chandāṃsi
34.4.11	chandobhir devā asurāṇāṃ chandāṃsy avṛñjata
34.4.12	chandobhir evaiṣāṃ chandāṃṣi vṛṅkte
34.4.13	sajanyaṃ śasyaṃ vihavyaṃ śasyam agastyasya kayāśubhīyaṃ śasyam
34.4.14	etāvad vāvāsti
34.4.15	yāvad evāsty antarikṣād divaḥ pṛthivyā ahorātrābhyāṃ tebhya enān sarvebhyo nirbhajati
34.4.16	yadi prātassavane kalaśo dīryeta vaiṣṇavīṣu śipiviṣṭavatīṣu mādhyandine pavamāne stuyuḥ
34.4.17	yad vai yajñasyātiricyate viṣṇuṃ tac chipiviṣṭam abhyatiricyate
34.4.18	atiriktaṃ vā etad atiriktaṃ śipiviṣṭam
34.4.19	atiriktenaivātiriktam āpnoti
34.4.20	yadi madhyandina ārbhavasya pavamānasya purastād vaṣaṭkāranidhanaṃ sāma kuryuḥ
34.4.21	yadi tṛtīyasavana etad eva
34.4.22	vaṣaṭkāro vai yajñasya pratiṣṭhā
34.4.23	pratiṣṭhām evainaṃ gamayanti
34.5.1	āsandīm āruhyodgātā mahāvratenodgāyati
34.5.2	preṅkham āruhya hotā mahad uktham anuśaṃsati
34.5.3	adhiṣṭhāne 'dhiṣṭhāyādhvaryū pratigṛṇītaḥ
34.5.4	kūrceṣv itara āsate
34.5.5	antarikṣaṃ vā annam
34.5.6	amuto vai pradīyate
34.5.7	asyāṃ prajāyate
34.5.8	tad antarikṣāya jāyate
34.5.9	yad antarikṣa āsīnā mahāvratena caranty annādyasyopāptyai
34.5.10	atho devasākṣya evopariṣadyaṃ jayanti
34.5.11	svargam u lokam ākramamāṇā yanti
34.5.12	abhigarāpagarau bhavataḥ
34.5.13	pra vā anyas sattriṇaś śaṃsati nindaty anyo yaḥ praśaṃsati
34.5.14	yad evaiṣāṃ suṣṭutaṃ suśastaṃ tat sa praśaṃsati
34.5.15	atha yo nindati yad evaiṣāṃ duṣṣtutaṃ duśśastaṃ tat so 'pahanti
34.5.16	śūdrāryau carman vyāyacchete
34.5.17	devāś ca vā asurāś cāditye vyāyacchanta
34.5.18	taṃ devā abhyajayan
34.5.19	āryaṃ varṇam ujjāpayati
34.5.20	ātmānam evojjāpayati
34.5.21	antarvedy āryas syād bahirvedi śūdraḥ
34.5.22	śvetaṃ carma parimaṇḍalaṃ syāt
34.5.23	ādityasya rūpam
34.5.24	sarvāsu sraktiṣu dundubhayo vadanti
34.5.25	yā dikṣu vāk tāṃ tenāvarundhate
34.5.26	bhūmidundubhir bhavati
34.5.27	yāsyāṃ vāk tāṃ tenāvarundhate
34.5.28	vīṇā vadanti
34.5.29	yā paśuṣu vāk tāṃ tenāvarundhate
34.5.30	kāṇḍavīṇā vadanti
34.5.31	yauṣadhiṣu vāk tāṃ tenāvarundhate
34.5.32	nāḍītūṇavā vadanti
34.5.33	yā vanaspatiṣu vāk tāṃ tenāvarundhate
34.5.34	vāṇaś śatatantur bhavati
34.5.35	śatāyur vai puruṣaś śatavīryaḥ
34.5.36	āyur eva vīryam avarunddhe
34.5.37	brahmacārī ca puṃśacalī cartīyete
34.5.38	sarvā hi bhūte vāco vadanti
34.5.39	mithunaṃ caranti
34.5.40	saṃvatsaraṃ vā ete prajāyamānās sattram āsate
34.5.41	teṣāṃ saṃvatsareṇaiva prajananam antardhīyate
34.5.42	yan mithunaṃ caranti saṃvatsarasyaiva prajananasyopāptyai
34.5.43	kumbhinīr upācaranti samṛddhyai
34.5.44	idaṃmadhuraṃ gāyantīs saṃnaddhakavacāḥ pariyanti
34.5.45	mahāvratam eva mahayanti
34.5.46	atho sendratāyā eva
34.5.47	brahmaṇo vā anyā tviṣiḥ kṣatrasyānyā
34.5.48	yad dīkṣito 'dhikṛṣṇājinas sā brahmaṇas tviṣiḥ
34.5.49	yat saṃnaddhakavaco 'dhijyadhanus sā kṣatrasya tviṣiḥ
34.5.50	tad ubhayaṃ bhavaty ubhayos tviṣyor avaruddhyai
34.6.1	prajāpatir vā ātmano 'dhi dvādaśāhaṃ niramimīta
34.6.2	saṃvatsaraḥ prajāpatiḥ
34.6.3	sa caturṇāṃ māsāṃ tisrastisro rātrīr ādatta
34.6.4	sā dīkṣābhavat
34.6.5	sa uttareṣāṃ caturṇāṃ tisrastisro rātrīr ādatta
34.6.6	tā upasado 'bhavan
34.6.7	sa uttareṣāṃ caturṇāṃ tisrastisro rātrīr ādatta
34.6.8	sā sutyābhavat
34.6.9	tasmād āhur yāvān saṃvatsaras tāvān dvādaśāha iti
34.6.10	sarvasmāddhy eṣa saṃvatsarād adhi nirmitaḥ
34.6.11	sa prathamaṃ cāhar asṛjatehīḍaṃ ca sāmemaṃ lokam agniṃ jyotiḥ
34.6.12	dvitīyaṃ cāhar asṛjatordhveḍaṃ ca sāmāntarikṣaṃ lokaṃ vāyuṃ jyotiḥ
34.6.13	tṛtīyaṃ cāhar asṛjateḍābhir aiḍaṃ ca sāmāmuṃ lokaṃ sūryaṃ jyotiḥ
34.6.14	caturthaṃ cāhar asṛjata paristubdheḍaṃ ca sāma yasmiṃś ca loke tejo jyotiḥ
34.6.15	pañcamaṃ cāhar asṛjatādhyardheḍaṃ ca sāma yasmiṃl loke satyaṃ jyotiḥ
34.6.16	ṣaṣṭhaṃ cāhar asṛjata hoiḍaṃ ca sāma yasmiṃl loke brahma jyotiḥ
34.6.17	saptamaṃ cāhar asṛjata punarnitunnāṃ ceḍāṃ yasmiṃś ca loke tapo jyotiḥ
34.6.18	aṣṭamaṃ cāhar asṛjata viṣvagaiḍaṃ ca sāma yasmiṃś ca loka ṛtaṃ jyotiḥ
34.6.19	navamaṃ cāhar asṛjata hoiḍaṃ ca sāma yasmiṃś ca loke brahma jyotiḥ
34.6.20	daśamaṃ cāhar asṛjata dvīḍaṃ ca sāma yasmiṃl loke 'mṛtaṃ jyotiḥ
34.6.21	prāṇa eva prāyaṇīyo 'pāna udayanīyaḥ
34.6.22	tasmād yāvad eva prāyaṇīye kriyate tāvad udayanīye kriyate
34.6.23	yāvān hi prāṇas tāvān apānaḥ
34.6.24	etāṃl lokān etāni sāmāny etāni jyotīṃṣy etāni tejāṃsy avarunddhe ya evaṃ vidvān dvādaśāhena yajate
34.7.1	prajāpatir akāmayata prajās sṛjeyeti
34.7.2	sa etam ātman dvādaśāham apaśyat
34.7.3	tam ātmano niramimīta
34.7.4	tena prajā asṛjata
34.7.5	taṃ gāyatrī chando 'nvasṛjyata
34.7.6	sākāmayatāham imaṃ sarvataḥ paribhaveyam iti
34.7.7	taṃ tejasā mukhataḥ paryabhavad ojasā madhyataś chandasopariṣṭāt
34.7.8	sarvato vai sā taṃ vyatyaśayat
34.7.9	sarvato bhrātṛvyaṃ vyatiśaye ya evaṃ veda
34.7.10	dve rūpe saṃvatsarasya māsā anyad ṛtavo 'nyat
34.7.11	yat ṣaḍ ṛtavas tenāptaḥ
34.7.12	yad dvādaśa māsās tenāptaḥ
34.7.13	ubhābhyām eva rūpābhyāṃ saṃvatsaram āpnoti
34.7.14	brahma vai gāyatrī
34.7.15	kṣatraṃ dvādaśāhaḥ
34.7.16	anv enaṃ kṣatraṃ budhyate
34.7.17	pra purodhām āpnoti ya evaṃ veda
34.7.18	yajñaṃ vā anyāni cchandāṃsy abhyasṛjyanta
34.7.19	svārājyam eva bṛhaty abhyasṛjyata
34.7.20	tasmād bṛhatyā na vaṣaṭkurvanti
34.7.21	yad vaṣaṭkuryuḥ paśūn agnau pradadhyuḥ
34.7.22	vacasāptvā paśūn avarundhate
34.7.23	vāci vā ete catvāraḥ paśavo gaur aśvo 'jāviḥ
34.7.24	tasmād vācā hūtāḥ paśava udāyanti
34.7.25	vācā siddhā āvartante
34.7.26	bṛhatīṃ vā eta āpnuvanti ya etā rātrīr āsate
34.7.27	ṣaṭtriṃśad etā rātrayaḥ
34.7.28	ṣaṭtriṃśadakṣarā bṛhatī
34.7.29	bṛhatī svargaṃ lokaṃ praveda
34.7.30	svargaṃ lokam āpnuvanti ya etā rātrīr āsate
34.7.31	devalokān vā eta āpnuvanti ya etā rātrīr āsate
34.7.32	ṣaṭtriṃśad etā rātrayaḥ
34.7.33	ṣaṭtriṃśad devalokāḥ
34.7.34	aṣṭau vasavaḥ
34.7.35	ekādaśa rudrāḥ
34.7.36	dvādaśādityāḥ
34.7.37	vaṣaṭkāraś ca prajāpatiś ca
34.7.38	traya ime lokāḥ
34.7.39	tān sarvān devalokān āpnuvanti ya etā rātrīr āsate
34.7.40	ubhaye vai devāś ca manuṣyāś cāvyāvṛttā āsan
34.7.41	te devā etaṃ dvādaśāham upāyan
34.7.42	te dīkṣayaivātmānam apunata
34.7.43	upasadbhir yajñaṃ samabharanta
34.7.44	hitvā śarīraṃ sutyayā svargaṃ lokam āyan
34.7.45	ya evaṃ vidvān dvādaśāham upaiti dīkṣayaivātmānaṃ punīta upasadbhir yajñaṃ saṃbharate hitvā śarīraṃ sutyayā svargaṃ lokam eti
34.7.46	prajāpatir vā etaṃ svargakāma āharat
34.7.47	sa na prābhavat
34.7.48	ekādaśāho vā eṣa
34.7.49	sa etam atirātram upariṣṭād ubhayataḥ paryaharat
34.7.50	samāno vā eṣa ubhayataḥ parihriyate svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
34.8.1	prajāpatir akāmayata prajāyeyeti
34.8.2	sa dvādaśāhenāyajata
34.8.3	tena prājāyata
34.8.4	praiva jāyate ya evaṃ veda
34.8.5	āpo vai yad yajñiyā medhyā asṛjyanta tad ekā api nāsṛjyanta
34.8.6	asṛg vāva tan nāsṛjyata
34.8.7	tad asno 'sṛktvam
34.8.8	tasmād yad evāsṛk chidyate 'tha yajñiyo medhyo bhavati
34.8.9	puruṣasaṃmito vā eṣa yas sattriyaṃ pratigṛhṇāti
34.8.10	puruṣaṃ vai so 'tti
34.8.11	yaṃ khalu vai puruṣam atti na tasyāsmiṃl loke nāmuṣminn apibhavati
34.8.12	prāṇo vai pūrvo 'tirātro 'pāna uttaraḥ
34.8.13	iyaṃ vai pūrvo 'tirātro 'sā uttaraḥ
34.8.14	agnir vai pūrvo 'gniṣṭomaḥ sūrya uttaraḥ
34.8.15	antarau vā etā anayoḥ
34.8.16	tasmād antarau prayujyete
34.8.17	tad āhur yad agniṣṭomaprāyaṇo yajñaḥ kasmād atirātrau pūrvau prayujyete iti
34.8.18	athāhuś cakṣuṣī vā ete yajñasya yad atirātrau kanīnike agniṣṭomā iti
34.8.19	yad agniṣṭomau pūrvau prayuñjīran bahiṣkanīnike nirādadhyur andhāḥ prajāyeran
34.8.20	yad atirātrau pūrvau prayujyete
34.8.21	cakṣuṣī eva yajñasya pratidhāya madhyataḥ kanīnike pratidadhāti
34.8.22	bhūtaṃ vai pūrvo 'tirātro bhavyam uttaraḥ
34.8.23	sad imāni daśāhāni madhye
34.8.24	sad bhavati ya evaṃ veda
34.8.25	yo ha vai gāyatrīṃ jyotiṣpakṣāṃ veda jyotiṣmatā bhāsā svargaṃ lokam eti
34.8.26	yā atirātrau tau pakṣau
34.8.27	yā agniṣṭomau te jyotiṣī
34.8.28	ye 'ṣṭā antara ukthyās sa ātmā
34.8.29	eṣā vai gāyatrī jyotiṣpakṣā
34.8.30	ya evaṃ gāyatrīṃ jyotiṣpakṣāṃ veda jyotiṣmatā bhāsā svargaṃ lokam eti
34.8.31	pakṣiṇo vā ete bhavanti
34.8.32	pakṣiṇo bhūtvā yatra kāmayanti tat parāpātam āsate
34.8.33	eṣa vai prajāpatir dvādaśadhā vinihito yad dvādaśāhaḥ
34.8.34	yā atirātrau tau pakṣau
34.8.35	yā agniṣṭomau te cakṣuṣī
34.8.36	ye 'ṣṭā antara ukthyās sa ātmā
34.8.37	sa eṣa prajāpatir eva
34.8.38	sad vai sattriṇas spṛṇvanti
34.8.39	tat sattrasya sattratvam
34.8.40	prāṇā vai sat
34.8.41	prāṇān eva tat spṛṇvanti
34.8.42	sarvāsāṃ vā ete prajānāṃ prāṇair āsate ye sattram āsate
34.8.43	tasmāt pṛcchanti kim ete sattriṇa iti
34.8.44	priyaḥ prajānām utthito bhavati ya evaṃ veda
34.9.1	prajāpatir akāmayata syām iti
34.9.2	sa dvādaśāhenāyajata
34.9.3	tenābhavat
34.9.4	tasmād āhur bubhūṣato yajña iti
34.9.5	taṃ māsā dīkṣitam adīkṣitā ayājayan
34.9.6	tasmād dīkṣitam adīkṣitā yājayanti
34.9.7	tebhya iṣam ūrjam adadāt
34.9.8	seyaṃ māseṣv ārdhnot prajāpatidattā
34.9.9	ārdhnuvan māsāḥ pratigṛhya
34.9.10	ṛdhnoti ya evaṃ vidvān dadāti
34.9.11	ṛdhnoti yaḥ pratigṛhṇāti
34.9.12	pīvā dīkṣeta
34.9.13	yad asyāṅgānāṃ mīyate juhoty eva tat
34.9.14	sa yathā vasanto navadāvyaś śobhamāna uttiṣṭhaty evam eva navadāvyaś śobhamāna uttiṣṭhati
34.9.15	tapo vai yajñasya śleṣma
34.9.16	yathā vai rathasya śleṣmaivaṃ yajñasya tapaḥ
34.9.17	yo 'tapasvī bhavaty asaṃśliṣṭo 'sya yajñaḥ
34.9.18	tapasvī syāt
34.9.19	yajñam eva saṃśleṣayate
34.9.20	ardhamāsā vāvāsan
34.9.21	te 'kāmayanta māsās syāmeti
34.9.22	te dvādaśāham upāyan
34.9.23	trayodaśaṃ brahmāṇaṃ kṛtvā tasmin dṛṣṭvodatiṣṭhan
34.9.24	tasmāt so 'nāyatana itarān upajīvati
34.9.25	tasmād dvādaśāhasya trayodaśena na brahmaṇā bhavitavyam
34.9.26	dvādaśa dīkṣeran saṃvatsarāyatanāḥ
34.9.27	dvādaśa māsās saṃvatsaraḥ
34.9.28	saṃvatsarāyatanā evardhnuvanti
34.9.29	trayodaśa dīkṣeran saṃvatsarāyatanāḥ
34.9.30	trayodaśa māsās saṃvatsaraḥ
34.9.31	saṃvatsarāyatanā evardhnuvanti
34.9.32	pañcadaśa dīkṣerann ardhamāsāyatanāḥ
34.9.33	pañcadaśārdhamāsasya rātrayaḥ
34.9.34	ardhamāsāyatanā evardhnuvanti
34.9.35	saptadaśa dīkṣeran prājāpatyāyatanāḥ
34.9.36	prajāpatis saptadaśa
34.9.37	prājāpatyāyatanā evardhnuvanti
34.9.38	ekāviṃśatir dīkṣeran rukkāmāḥ
34.9.39	asā āditya ekaviṃśaḥ
34.9.40	eṣa rucaḥ pradātā
34.9.41	sa ebhyo rucaṃ prayacchati
34.9.42	caturviṃśatir dīkṣeran brahmavarcasakāmāḥ
34.9.43	caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī
34.9.44	tejo gāyatrī brahmavarcasam
34.9.45	teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhate
34.9.46	saptaviṃśatir dīkṣeraṃs triṇavāyatanāḥ
34.9.47	triṇavā ime lokāḥ
34.9.48	triṇavāyatanā evardhnuvanti
34.9.49	triṃśad dīkṣeran māsāyatanāḥ
34.9.50	triṃśan māso rātrayaḥ
34.9.51	māsāyatanā evardhnuvanti
34.9.52	trayastriṃśad dīkṣeran devatāyatanāḥ
34.9.53	trayastriṃśad devatāḥ
34.9.54	devatāyatanā evardhnuvanti
34.9.55	catuścatvāriṃśad dīkṣerann ojaskāmā vīryakāmāḥ
34.9.56	caturścatvāriṃśadakṣarā triṣṭubh
34.9.57	ojo vīryaṃ triṣṭup
34.9.58	oja eva vīryam avarundhate
34.9.59	aṣṭācatvāriṃśad dīkṣeran paśukāmāḥ
34.9.60	aṣṭācatvāriṃśadakṣarā jagatī
34.9.61	jāgatāḥ paśavaḥ
34.9.62	paśūn evāvarundhate
34.9.63	aparimitā dīkṣerann aparimitasyāvaruddhyai
34.9.64	aparimitaḥ prajāpatiḥ
34.9.65	prajāpatim evāpnuvanti
34.9.66	ṛtavo vāvāsann anuyāvarā māsāḥ
34.9.67	te māsā akāmayantartūn āpnuyāmeti
34.9.68	te dvādaśāham upāyan
34.9.69	trayodaśaṃ brahmāṇaṃ kṛtvā ta ṛtūñ chiśireṇa nibhāyya vasantam ūrjam eṣām abhyudatiṣṭhan
34.9.70	ya evaṃ vidvāñ chiśire dīkṣate tapasaiva bhrātṛvyaṃ nibhāyyeṣam ūrjam asyābhyuttiṣṭhati
34.9.71	śiśiraṃ vā etasya prayāṇam
34.9.72	vasanto 'vasānam

34.17.1	yathā vai ratha ekaikam aram abhipratitiṣṭhan vartata evaṃ yajña ekaikāṃ tanvam abhipratitiṣṭhann eti
34.17.2	purā pracaritor āgnīdhre hotavyāḥ
34.17.3	etad dha vā uvāca vāsiṣṭhas sātyahavyaḥ
34.17.4	askān soma ity ukte mā sūrkṣata pracarata prātar vāvādyāhaṃ somaṃ samasthāpayam iti
34.17.5	nāsya somas skandati ya evaṃ veda
34.17.6	sa ha sma vai sa āsandyām āsīnas saktubhir upamathya somaṃ pibati
34.17.7	ahaṃ vāva sarvato yajñaṃ veda
34.17.8	ya etā veda na mām eṣa hiṃsiṣyatīti
34.17.9	nainaṃ somaḥ pīto na peyo hinasti ya evaṃ vidvān somaṃ pibati
34.17.10	taṃ ha sma yad āhuḥ kasmāt tvam idam āsīnas saktubhir upamathya somaṃ pibasīti
34.17.11	devatāsv eva yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayāmīty abravīt
34.17.12	yasyaivaṃ viduṣo yasyaivaṃ vidvān yajñārtyā yajñaprāyaścittiṃ juhoti devatāsv eva yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
34.17.13	yajñārtiṃ pratijuhuyāt sayonitvāya
34.17.14	trayastriṃśad vai yajñasya tanvaḥ
34.17.15	ekānnatriṃśat stomabhāgās trīṇi savanāni yajñaś caturthaḥ
34.17.16	stomabhāgair evaitat stomabhāgān pratiyuṅkte savanais savanāni yajñena yajñam
34.17.17	sarvā ha vā asya yajñasya tanvaḥ prayuktā bhavanti sarvā āptāḥ sarvā avaruddhāḥ
34.17.18	devasya savituḥ prasave bṛhaspataye stuteti
34.17.19	yadyad vai savitā devebhyaḥ prāsuvat tenārdhnuvan
34.17.20	savitṛprasūtā eva stuvanti
34.17.21	ṛdhnuvanti
34.17.22	ṛdhyante ha vā asya stomā ṛdhyate yajña ṛdhyate yajamānāyardhyate prajāyā ṛdhyate paśubhya ṛdhyate brahmaṇe yasyaivaṃ viduṣo yasyaivaṃ vidvān brahmā bhavati
34.18.1	yo vai stomabhāgānām āyatāś ca pratihitāś ca vidyāt sa samṛtasomasya brahmā syāt
34.18.2	bahiṣpavamāne prastute brūyāt
34.18.3	stuteṣe stutorje stuta devasya savituḥ prasave bṛhaspatiprasūtā iti
34.18.4	etā vai stomabhāgānām āyatapratihitāḥ
34.18.5	ya evaṃ vidyāt sa samṛtasomasya brahmā syāt
34.18.6	yāṃ diśaṃ somau saṃstutau syātāṃ tāṃ diśaṃ parīkṣeta
34.18.7	idam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putraṃ śucā vidhyāmīti
34.18.8	ṛtvijām ekaṃ brūyāt
34.18.9	śucaivainān vidhyati
34.18.10	yo vai stomabhāgānām āyatāś ca pratihitāś cāvidvān brahmā bhavati sa viṣvagvīryeṇa vyṛdhyate
34.18.11	bahiṣpavamāne prastute
34.18.12	stuteṣe stutorje stuta devasya savituḥ prasave bṛhaspatiprasūtā iti
34.18.13	uparyupari brahmāṇam atīkṣeta

34.18.18	abhūd devas savitā vandyo nu na idānīm ahna upavācyo nṛbhiḥ

34.18.20	abhimantrayeta

36.2.51	tān eva bhrātṛvyād yuvate

36.3.1	vaiśvadevena yajate prajākāmo vā paśukāmo vā na varuṇapraghāsair na sākamedhaiḥ
36.3.2	sarvo vai puruṣas sāhasro jāyate
36.3.3	yāvattarasaṃ tvai gacchati
36.3.4	prajananam etad dhavir yad vaiśvadevam
36.3.5	prajananam eva yajate svāṃ mātrāṃ gacchānīti
36.3.6	yadā sahasraṃ paśūn gacched atha varuṇapraghāsair yajeta
36.3.7	yad eva tat sahasram agaṃs tasyāṃho 'vayajate
36.3.8	ṛtuyājī vā anyaś cāturmāsyayājy anyaḥ
36.3.9	yo vasanto 'bhūt prāvṛd abhūc charad abhūd iti
36.3.10	yajate sa ṛtuyājī
36.3.11	yas trayodaśaṃ māsaṃ saṃpādayati sa trayodaśaṃ māsam abhiyajate sa cāturmāsyayājī
36.3.12	trīn ṛjūn iṣṭvā caturtham utsṛjet
36.3.13	dvau parā ṛjū iṣṭvā tṛtīyam utsṛjet
36.3.14	ye vai trayas saṃvatsarās teṣāṃ ṣaṭtriṃśat pūrṇamāsāḥ
36.3.15	yau dvau tayoś caturviṃśatiḥ
36.3.16	ye ṣaṭ triṃśaty adhi te caturviṃśatim upayanti
36.3.17	eṣa vāva sa trayodaśo māsaḥ
36.3.18	tam evaitat saṃpādayati
36.3.19	tam abhiyajate
36.3.20	yad barhiḥ prayājeṣu yajaty oṣadhīs tad yajati yad barhir anuyājeṣu
36.3.21	phalaṃ tad yajati
36.3.22	yad barhir vāritīnām
36.3.23	yad eva phalād adhi prajāyate tat tad yajati
36.3.24	yad duro yajaty upasthaṃ tad yajati
36.3.25	yad uṣāsānaktā vyuṣṭiṃ caiva nimruktiṃ ca tad yajati
36.3.26	yaj joṣṭrī yad eva jātaṃ yaj janiṣyamāṇaṃ tad yajati
36.3.27	yad ūrjāhutī yad evātti ca pibati ca tat tad yajati
36.3.28	yad daivyā hotārā ime vai daivyā hotārā
36.3.29	ime eva tad yajati
36.3.30	yat tisro devīr vāg vai tisro devīḥ
36.3.31	vācam eva tad yajati
36.3.32	chandāṃsi vai vāk
36.3.33	chandāṃsy eva tad yajati
36.3.34	narāśaṃsaṃ yajati
36.3.35	tanūnapād vai yajñaḥ prasṛtaḥ
36.3.36	narāśaṃso 'prasṛtaḥ
36.3.37	prasṛto vā etarhi yajñaḥ
36.3.38	tasmān narāśaṃsam anuyājeṣu yajati
36.3.39	tvaṣṭāraṃ yajati
36.3.40	sa hi rūpāṇi vikaroti
36.3.41	vanaspatiṃ yajati
36.3.42	ūrg vai somo vanaspatiḥ
36.3.43	saumīr imāḥ prajāḥ

36.4.1	vājino yajati
36.4.2	paśavo vai vājinaḥ

36.4.5	saṃsthite hi yajñe prahṛteṣu paridhiṣu juhoti

36.4.7	anuyajati

36.5.1	tā vaiśvadevena sṛṣṭās tasmiṃs taruṇiman varuṇo 'gṛhṇāt

36.5.36	anṛtaṃ strī

37.10.1	bodhaś ca mā pratībodhaś ca purastād gopāyatām / asvapnaś ca mānavadrāṇaś ca dakṣiṇato gopāyatām / gopāyamānaś ca mā rakṣamāṇaś ca paścād gopāyatām / jāgṛviś ca mārundhatī cottarād gopāyatām / anamitraṃ no adharāg anamitram udak kṛdhi / indrānamitraṃ naḥ paścād anamitraṃ puras kṛdhi
37.10.2	anamitrair ahobhis sacīmahi viśve devā anamitrā na uṣasas santu nimrucaḥ
37.10.3	yāṣ ṣaḍ urvīḥ pañca pradiśas tā naḥ pāntu / mitradhā no mitre dadhātā / abhayaṃ no astu / ye rātrīm anutiṣṭhatha ye ca bhūteṣu jāgṛtha / paśūn ye sarvān rakṣatha te na ātmasu jāgṛta

37.11.1	ye rāṣṭrabhṛto ye rāṣṭrasyānubhartāras tebhyo rāṣṭrīyaḥ parideyaḥ

37.14.1	devāś ca vā asurāś ca saṃyattā āsan
37.14.2	asureṣu tarhy amṛtam āsīc chuṣṇe dānave
37.14.3	tac chuṣṇa evāntar āsye 'bibhaḥ
37.14.4	yān devānām aghnaṃs tad eva te 'bhavan
37.14.5	yān asurāṇāṃ tāñ chuṣṇo 'mṛtenābhivyānīt
37.14.6	te samānan
37.14.7	sa indro 'vet
37.14.8	asureṣu vā amṛtaṃ śuṣṇe dānava iti
37.14.9	sa madhvaṣṭhīlā bhūtvā prapathe 'śayat
37.14.10	tāṃ śuṣṇo 'bhi vyādadāt
37.14.11	tasyendraś śyeno bhūtvāsyād amṛtaṃ niramathnāt
37.14.12	tasmād eṣa vayasāṃ vīryāvattamaḥ
37.14.13	indrasya hy eṣaikā tanūḥ
37.14.14	amṛtam eṣa bibharti ya evaṃ veda
37.14.15	yaṃ kāmayeta
37.14.16	āmayāvinaṃ jīved iti
37.14.17	taṃ vyādāyābhivyanyāt
37.14.18	amṛtenaivainam abhivyaniti
37.14.19	jīvati
37.14.20	sarvam āyur eti
37.14.21	na purāyuṣaḥ pramīyate
37.14.22	devāś ca vā asurāś ca saṃyattā āsan
37.14.23	te devā asurān aghnan
37.14.24	teṣāṃ ya udaśiṣyanta
37.14.25	te devān anvarohan
37.14.26	ta enān vṛñjānāḥ pratyasyamānā āyan
37.14.27	te devās samitim akurvata
37.14.28	ta etau brahmayātuṃ ca devayātuṃ cāpaśyan
37.14.29	tā ebhyaḥ pratyavāsṛjan
37.14.30	tā enān niradahatām
37.14.31	tā enān vṛñjānau pratyasyamānā aitām
37.14.32	teṣāṃ ye 'tyamucyanta te manuṣyān prāviśan
37.14.33	tajjanmāno yātudhānāḥ kravyāda itare
37.14.34	na ha vā asya yātudhānā na kravyādo na piśācā na rakṣāṃsīśate
37.14.35	nainaṃ śaptaṃ nābhicaritam āgacchati ya evaṃ veda
37.14.36	tad yady enaṃ yātudhāna iti brūyur nāpahnuvīta
37.14.37	etau hy eva tasya yātū
37.14.38	ko 'si katamo 'sīti
37.14.39	eṣa vai brahmayātuḥ
37.14.40	tasmā evainam apidadhāti
37.14.41	sa tvaṃ no deva gāyatreṇa cchandasāhne paripāhīti
37.14.42	ahna evātmānaṃ paridadāti
37.14.43	mṛḍo 'si mṛḍase dvipade catuṣpada iti
37.14.44	dvipadaś caivāsmai catuṣpadaś ca paśūn paridadāti
37.14.45	ādityo 'si vṛṣṇo aśvasya retaḥ
37.14.46	devānāṃ yātur asi
37.14.47	yātur me 'si
37.14.48	asumaddhitaṃ jahīti
37.14.49	eṣa vai devayātuḥ
37.14.50	tasmā evainam apidadhāti
37.14.51	sa tvaṃ no deva traiṣṭubhena cchandasā rātryai paripāhīti
37.14.52	rātryā evātmānaṃ paridadāti
37.14.53	mṛṇo 'si mṛṇāmuṣya dvipadaś catuṣpada iti
37.14.54	dvipadaś caivāsmai catuṣpadaś ca paśūn apidadhāti
37.14.55	skambho 'si
37.14.56	bleṣko 'sīti
37.14.57	etau vai yamaśvā ahaś ca rātrī ca
37.14.58	tā idaṃ manuṣyān vṛñjānau pratyasyamānā itaḥ
37.14.59	tābhyām evainam apidadhāti
37.14.60	tā enaṃ vṛñjānau pratyasyamānā itaḥ
37.14.61	yadā pravlayavyathita iva manyeta
37.14.62	agnaye vītamanyave svāheti juhuyāt
37.14.63	īśvaro vā abhicaro 'śāntaḥ pratyaṅṅ etoś śāntyai
37.16.1	yān vā asurā devebhyo nyadadhata tān devā anvapaśyan
37.16.2	yān devā asurebhyas tān asurā nānvapaśyan
37.16.3	tato devā abhavan
37.16.4	parāsurā abhavan
37.16.5	yatrānyo nānupaśyet tad etān nidadhīta
37.16.6	bhrātṛvyasyānanukśatyai
37.16.7	bhavaty ātmanā
37.16.8	parāsya bhrātṛvyo bhavati
37.16.9	pṛthivyai svāhāntarikṣāya svāhā dive svāheti
37.16.10	traya ime lokāḥ
37.16.11	ebhya evainaṃ lokebhyaḥ paridadāti
37.16.12	kāmāya svāheti
37.16.13	āyur vai paramaḥ kāmaḥ
37.16.14	āyur eva tena spṛṇoti
37.16.15	svapnāya svāheti
37.16.16	yā evainaṃ svapantaṃ nāṣṭrā dipsanti svapna enaṃ tābhyaḥ pāti
37.16.17	ahne svāhā rātryai svāheti
37.16.18	dvau vā ṛtū ahaś ca rātrī ca
37.16.19	tābhyām evainaṃ paridadāti
37.16.20	saptaitā āhutīr juhoti
37.16.21	sapta prāṇāḥ
37.16.22	tān evāsmin dadhāti
37.16.23	tān asminn adhi viyātayati
37.16.24	tān asmād anapagān karoti
37.16.25	ghṛtenāśmānam anakti
37.16.26	eṣa hy etarhy etasyātmā
37.16.27	tejo ghṛtam
37.16.28	yāvān evāsyātmā taṃ tejasānakti
37.16.29	sarvato 'nakti
37.16.30	sarvata evainaṃ tejasā samardhayati
37.16.31	tṛptas tvaṃ tṛpto 'ham iti
37.16.32	prāṇān evāsyaitan mahimno vyācaṣṭe
37.16.33	prāṇā hi mahimānaḥ
37.16.34	dyaur me pitā pṛthivī me mātā sūryo me cakṣur vāto me prāṇa iti
37.16.35	etābhya eva devatābhya ātmānaṃ paridadāti
37.16.36	astṛto nāmāham asmi sa idaṃ dyāvāpṛthivyor ātmānaṃ paridada iti
37.16.37	dyāvāpṛthivyor evātmānaṃ paridatte
37.16.38	tayoś śraye tayoḥ parākrama iti
37.16.39	yo vā anayoḥ parākramate na sa vyathate
37.16.40	anayor eva parākraṃsta
37.16.41	gopīthāya pipṛtaṃ mā mā mā hiṃsiṣṭam iti
37.16.42	ātmano 'hiṃsāyai
37.16.43	pāhi dviṣaḥ pāhi riṣaḥ pāhy adevyā abhiśastyā ity āśiṣam evāśāste
37.16.44	sarvato 'śmānaṃ pariharati
37.16.45	eṣa hy etaṃ sarvataḥ pātīyāntaṃ loṣṭam udrujati
37.16.46	etāvān hy ātmā
37.16.47	bāhumātram avaṭaṃ khanati
37.16.48	etāvān hi puruṣaḥ
37.16.49	tam avadhāyāthāśmānam atha hiraṇyam
37.16.50	asyā evainam uttarārdhe nidadhāti
37.16.51	anikhāto bhavati
37.16.52	nābhiṃ prati nikhanati
37.16.53	nābhir vai prāṇān dādhāra ye cordhvā ye cāvāñcaḥ prāṇānāṃ dhṛtyai
37.16.54	hiraṇyena saṃsparśayati
37.16.55	amṛtaṃ vai hiraṇyam
37.16.56	amṛtenaivainaṃ saṃdadhāti
37.16.57	ud vācam un manīṣām iti
37.16.58	etāni vā asya nikhanet tāny evoddharati
37.16.59	ātmamātrī vedir bhavati
37.16.60	ātmamātraṃ hi varma
37.16.61	yan nātmamātrī syān nātmane kriyeta
37.16.62	etāvatī pṛthivī yāvatī vediḥ
37.16.63	asyā evaitad anteṣu puro 'dhita
37.16.64	devapurā evākṛta
37.16.65	atho etā eva devatā etāsāṃ diśāṃ paraspā akṛta gopīthāya
37.17.1	ṛṣayo vā indraṃ pratyakṣaṃ nāpaśyan
37.17.2	taṃ vasiṣṭha eva pratyakṣam apaśyat
37.17.3	so 'bibhed itarebhyo marṣibhyaḥ pravakṣyatīti
37.17.4	so 'bravīd brāhmaṇaṃ te vakṣyāmi yathā tvatpurohitāḥ prajāḥ prajaniṣyante 'tha metarebhya ṛṣibhyo mā pravoca iti
37.17.5	tasmā etān stomabhāgān abravīt
37.17.6	tato vasiṣṭhapurohitāḥ prajāḥ prājāyanta
37.17.7	stomo vā eteṣāṃ bhāgaḥ
37.17.8	tat stomabhāgānāṃ stomabhāgatvam
37.17.9	raśmir asi
37.17.10	kṣayāya tvā
37.17.11	kṣayaṃ jinveti
37.17.12	kṣayo vai devāḥ
37.17.13	devebhya eva yajñaṃ prāha
37.17.14	pretir asi
37.17.15	dharmeṇa tvā
37.17.16	dharmaṃ jinveti
37.17.17	dharmo manuṣyāḥ
37.17.18	manuṣyebhya eva yajñaṃ prāha
37.17.19	anvitir asi
37.17.20	dive tvā
37.17.21	divaṃ jinva
37.17.22	saṃdhir asi
37.17.23	antarikṣāya tvā
37.17.24	antarikṣaṃ jinva
37.17.25	pratidhir asi
37.17.26	pṛthivyai tvā
37.17.27	pṛthivīṃ jinveti
37.17.28	traya ime lokāḥ
37.17.29	ebhya eva lokebhyo yajñaṃ prāha
37.17.30	viṣṭambho 'si
37.17.31	vṛṣṭyai tvā
37.17.32	vṛṣṭiṃ jinveti
37.17.33	vṛṣṭim evāvarunddhe
37.17.34	pravāsy anuvāsīti
37.17.35	mithunam eva karoti
37.17.36	uśig asi
37.17.37	vasubhyas tvā
37.17.38	vasūñ jinva
37.17.39	praketo 'si
37.17.40	rudrebhyas tvā
37.17.41	rudrāñ jinva
37.17.42	suditir asi
37.17.43	ādityebhyas tvā
37.17.44	ādityāñ jinveti
37.17.45	aṣṭau vasavaḥ
37.17.46	ekādaśa rudrāḥ
37.17.47	dvādaśādityāḥ
37.17.48	vāg dvātriṃśī
37.17.49	svaras trayastriṃśaḥ
37.17.50	trayastriṃśad devatāḥ
37.17.51	devatābhya eva yajñaṃ prāha
37.17.52	ojo 'si
37.17.53	pitṛbhyas tvā
37.17.54	pitṝñ jinveti
37.17.55	devān eva pitṝn anusaṃtanoti
37.17.56	tantur asi
37.17.57	prajābhyas tvā
37.17.58	prajā jinveti
37.17.59	prajā eva paśūn anusaṃtanoti
37.17.60	pṛtanāṣāḍ asi
37.17.61	paśubhyas tvā
37.17.62	paśūñ jinveti
37.17.63	prajā eva paśūn anusaṃtanoti
37.17.64	revad asi
37.17.65	oṣadhībhyas tvā
37.17.66	oṣadhīr jinveti
37.17.67	oṣadhīṣv eva paśūn pratiṣṭhāpayati
37.17.68	abhijid asi yuktagrāvā
37.17.69	indrāya tvā
37.17.70	indraṃ jinveti
37.17.71	vajro vai ṣoḍaśī
37.17.72	vyāvṛtto 'nyair vajraḥ
37.17.73	tasmād eṣo 'nyair vyāvṛttaḥ
37.17.74	adhipatir asi
37.17.75	prāṇāya tvā
37.17.76	prāṇaṃ jinveti
37.17.77	prāṇam evāvarunddhe
37.17.78	dharuṇo 'si
37.17.79	apānāya tvā
37.17.80	apānaṃ jinveti
37.17.81	apānam evāvarunddhe
37.17.82	saṃsarpo 'si
37.17.83	cakṣuṣe tvā
37.17.84	cakṣur jinveti
37.17.85	cakṣur evāvarunddhe
37.17.86	vayodhā asi
37.17.87	śrotrāya tvā
37.17.88	śrotraṃ jinveti
37.17.89	śrotram evāvarunddhe
37.17.90	etad vai puruṣam akaḥ
37.17.91	athātaḥ prāṇān upaiti
37.17.92	prajāpatim eva
37.17.93	trivṛd asi
37.17.94	trivṛte tvā
37.17.95	savṛd asi
37.17.96	savṛte tvā
37.17.97	pravṛd asi
37.17.98	pravṛte tvā
37.17.99	anūvṛd asi
37.17.100	anūvṛte tveti
37.17.101	mithunam eva karoti
37.17.102	saṃroho 'si
37.17.103	viroho 'si
37.17.104	praroho 'si
37.17.105	anūroho 'sīti
37.17.106	prajāpatir eva
37.17.107	vasuko 'si
37.17.108	vasyaṣṭir asi
37.17.109	veṣaśrīr asīti
37.17.110	pratiṣṭhir eva
37.17.111	devasya savituḥ prasave bṛhaspataye stuteti
37.17.112	yad yad vai savitā devebhyaḥ prāsuvat tenārdhnuvan
37.17.113	savitṛprasūtā eva stuvanti
37.17.114	ṛdhnuvanti yasyaivaṃ viduṣo yasyaivaṃ vidvān stomabhāgair brahmā bhavati vasīyān bhavati
